					<item>
				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics and LG Uplus Collaborate on ISAC Technology for 6G]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-electronics-and-lg-uplus-collaborate-on-isac-technology-for-6g</link>
				<pubDate>Fri, 29 May 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/28094305/Samsung-Corporate-Integrated-Sensing-and-Communication-6G-LG-Uplus-MoU_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Technology]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[6G]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Integrated Sensing and Communication]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[ISAC]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[LG Uplus]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4uCOOLU</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics and LG Uplus signed a memorandum of understanding (MOU) to jointly research Integrated Sensing and Communication (ISAC) technology at LG Science Park in Magok, Seoul, on May 27. Samsung Research, the advanced R&D hub within Samsung’s Device eXperience (DX) Division, will lead development efforts aimed at securing core technologies for the 6G era. […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/28094007/Samsung-Corporate-Integrated-Sensing-and-Communication-6G-LG-Uplus-MoU_main1.jpg" alt="(From left) Sangyeob Lee, CTO and Senior Vice President at LG Uplus and JinGuk Jeong, Executive Vice President and Head of the Advanced Communications Research Center (ACRC), Samsung Research at Samsung Electronics" class="wp-image-174441" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ (From left) Sangyeob Lee, CTO and Senior Vice President at LG Uplus and JinGuk Jeong, Executive Vice President and Head of the Advanced Communications Research Center (ACRC), Samsung Research at Samsung Electronics</figcaption></figure>



<p>Samsung Electronics and LG Uplus signed a memorandum of understanding (MOU) to jointly research Integrated Sensing and Communication (ISAC) technology at LG Science Park in Magok, Seoul, on May 27. Samsung Research, the advanced R&D hub within Samsung’s Device eXperience (DX) Division, will lead development efforts aimed at securing core technologies for the 6G era.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Wireless Sensing With Existing Networks</strong></h2>



<p>ISAC technology leverages existing communications infrastructure to collect information about surrounding environments without the need for dedicated equipment. By analyzing wireless signals transmitted by base stations and other network devices as they reflect off nearby objects, ISAC can detect an object’s speed, distance and direction of movement.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="500" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/28151609/Samsung-Corporate-Integrated-Sensing-and-Communication-6G-LG-Uplus-MoU_main2_FINAL.jpg" alt="ISAC-based sensing methods" class="wp-image-174478" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ ISAC-based sensing methods</figcaption></figure>



<p>Traditionally, environmental sensing required dedicated equipment such as light detection and ranging (LiDAR)<sup data-fn="b8b84113-e4e2-453f-b560-80419db5bcda" class="fn"><a href="#b8b84113-e4e2-453f-b560-80419db5bcda" id="b8b84113-e4e2-453f-b560-80419db5bcda-link">1</a></sup> or radio detection and ranging (radar)<sup data-fn="f43f4af5-a402-4ced-a507-a66e23eca95c" class="fn"><a href="#f43f4af5-a402-4ced-a507-a66e23eca95c" id="f43f4af5-a402-4ced-a507-a66e23eca95c-link">2</a></sup> sensors. ISAC, however, enables sensing using existing communications infrastructure including cellular and Wi-Fi networks. The International Telecommunication Union Radiocommunication Sector (ITU-R), a global telecommunications standards body, has designated ISAC as one of the three key usage scenarios for 6G.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Improving Safety and Operational Efficiency</strong></h2>



<p>ISAC technology is gaining industry attention for its wide range of applications across indoor and outdoor environments, from everyday settings to industrial sites. It can detect human movement in safety-related situations, track drones and robots, and monitor traffic congestion and weather changes.</p>



<p>By leveraging wireless signals, ISAC can identify objects beyond a camera’s field of view and in low-light or nighttime conditions. These capabilities could enable new services that improve safety, efficiency and productivity in consumer and industrial sectors.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Real-World Testing and Multimodal AI Development</strong></h2>



<p>To explore these possibilities, the two companies plan to identify ISAC-based use cases and validate the technology’s performance on existing 5G networks and in the 7 GHz band — a candidate frequency for 6G — to assess the feasibility of real-world deployment.</p>



<p>Initially, the collaboration will focus on enhancing everyday safety through human detection and improving network operational efficiency. Over time, the companies plan to expand the research by combining ISAC-generated wireless data — such as location, speed and density information — with camera imagery to further improve detection accuracy. To support these efforts, they will also develop multimodal AI technologies that integrate and analyze diverse forms of sensing data — including images, audio and video.</p>



<p>Under the partnership, Samsung Research will develop core ISAC and AI-driven 6G technologies, while LG Uplus will lead validation including data provision and field-testing infrastructure setup, based on its extensive experience in mobile network operations.</p>



<p>“ISAC is a core technology that transforms communications networks into sensing platforms, enabling users, network operators and industries to experience the full value of 6G,” said JinGuk Jeong, Executive Vice President and Head of the Advanced Communications Research Center (ACRC), Samsung Research at Samsung Electronics. “Through our collaboration with LG Uplus, we will validate the potential of 6G services across a range of real-world environments and continue advancing key 6G technologies.”</p>



<p>“In the 6G era, it will be increasingly important to verify how research technologies perform in real-world communication networks,” said Sangyeob Lee, CTO and Senior Vice President at LG Uplus. “Through our collaboration with Samsung Research, we aim to validate these technologies from a mobile network operator’s perspective and steadily strengthen our capabilities for future communication technologies.”</p>



<p>Following the publication of its <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-electronics-unveils-6g-white-paper-and-outlines-direction-for-ai-native-and-sustainable-communication" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">6G white paper</a> outlining the company’s vision for next-generation communications, Samsung has continued strengthening its 6G industry collaboration, including joint technology demonstrations with its global partners at the Silicon Valley Future Wireless Summit in November 2025 and the AI-RAN Alliance at Mobile World Congress (MWC) in March 2026. Moving forward, the company will continue advancing core 6G technologies to enable safer, smarter and more efficient everyday experiences.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="b8b84113-e4e2-453f-b560-80419db5bcda">A technology that uses laser light to measure distance. <a href="#b8b84113-e4e2-453f-b560-80419db5bcda-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="f43f4af5-a402-4ced-a507-a66e23eca95c">A technology that uses radio waves to measure distance and speed. <a href="#f43f4af5-a402-4ced-a507-a66e23eca95c-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 2"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li></ol>]]></content:encoded>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung and Massachusetts General Hospital Launch Joint Study To Investigate GLP-1 Treatment Monitoring With Galaxy Watch]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-and-massachusetts-general-hospital-launch-joint-study-to-investigate-glp-1-treatment-monitoring-with-galaxy-watch</link>
				<pubDate>Thu, 28 May 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/27151013/Samsung-Mobile-Massachusetts-General-Hospital-GLP-1-Treatment-Galaxy-Watch_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Mobile]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Release]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[BioActive Sensor]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Galaxy Watch]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Galaxy Watch Series]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Galaxy Watch8]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/3Q2kRG0</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics and Massachusetts General Hospital (MGH) Diabetes Research Center (DRC) today jointly announced a research study to investigate the efficacy of Galaxy Watch in assisting adults starting GLP-1RA therapy to monitor and potentially manage muscle loss. With nearly one in five adults in the US saying they have taken GLP-1 medication, this innovative clinical […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics and Massachusetts General Hospital (MGH) Diabetes Research Center (DRC) today jointly announced a research study to investigate the efficacy of Galaxy Watch in assisting adults starting GLP-1RA<sup data-fn="a6948455-d22d-439b-b090-6b340c841573" class="fn"><a href="#a6948455-d22d-439b-b090-6b340c841573" id="a6948455-d22d-439b-b090-6b340c841573-link">1</a></sup> therapy to monitor and potentially manage muscle loss. With <a href="https://www.kff.org/public-opinion/poll-1-in-8-adults-say-they-are-currently-taking-a-glp-1-drug-for-weight-loss-diabetes-or-another-condition-even-as-half-say-the-drugs-are-difficult-to-afford/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">nearly one in five adults in the US saying they have taken GLP-1 medication</a>, this innovative clinical study will investigate how continuous data from Galaxy Watch can help patients and clinicians monitor and mitigate muscle loss by providing a clearer, more holistic view of a person’s body composition and activity levels during treatment.</p>



<p>As GLP-1 medications become widely adopted for weight management and chronic disease treatment, tracking changes in muscle mass and physical activity alongside weight loss has emerged as a key medical focus. This research will delve into the feasibility of managing muscle loss for GLP-1 patients by utilizing biometric data including body composition, activity levels and heart rate provided by Galaxy Watch and Samsung Health.</p>



<p>Samsung and MGH have continuously collaborated on digital health research utilizing both Galaxy Watch and Samsung Health, including studies on Advanced Glycation End Products (AGEs). The MGH Diabetes Research Center, which specializes in research on diabetes and GLP-1 obesity treatment, initiated the joint study with Samsung after recognizing the potential for wearables to monitor body composition.</p>



<p>This study will also utilize Galaxy Watch8, powered by Samsung’s groundbreaking BioActive Sensor,<sup data-fn="a81a318c-73f3-4057-b456-f4bf42275456" class="fn"><a href="#a81a318c-73f3-4057-b456-f4bf42275456" id="a81a318c-73f3-4057-b456-f4bf42275456-link">2</a></sup> which helps provide advanced predictive and preventative wellness through more accurate health measurements.</p>



<p>Under the leadership of Dr. Melissa Putman, the study will enroll 100 adults beginning treatment with weight-loss medications into two groups. The intervention group will use Galaxy Watch to monitor their body composition via Bioelectrical Impedance Analysis (BIA), track physical activity and receive personalized exercise guides. Their progress will be compared to the other group, which will receive the standard guidance and care typically given to patients starting GLP-1RA therapy.</p>



<p>To evaluate the study’s progress, researchers will use clinical-grade DXA scans<sup data-fn="c186ca08-5a50-4a22-bca4-b759d1d3255e" class="fn"><a href="#c186ca08-5a50-4a22-bca4-b759d1d3255e" id="c186ca08-5a50-4a22-bca4-b759d1d3255e-link">3</a></sup> — the gold standard for body composition analysis — to track physiological changes in both groups. These data will help determine whether the insights and tailored guidance provided by Galaxy Watch8 can effectively support participants in building healthier daily habits, which may in turn contribute to better health outcomes particularly in preserving muscle mass.</p>



<p>“Many GLP-1 patients struggle with muscle mass loss, a common side effect that can cause an increased risk of cardiovascular disease and a drop in basal metabolic rate, which can lead to future weight regain,” said Dr. Putman, Director of the MGH Diabetes Research Center. “We’re interested in exploring how continuous data from a wearable device can provide invaluable insights into a patient’s activity levels, heart rate and body composition, giving clinicians a more holistic view of treatment impact and allowing for more timely, data-driven adjustments to their care plan.”</p>



<p>“This collaboration with MGH focuses on addressing real-world health challenges that patients face during GLP-1RA therapy, specifically managing muscle loss and building healthy habits,” said Jongmin Choi, Head of Health R&D Group, Mobile eXperience (MX) Business, Samsung Electronics. “Ultimately, this study highlights Samsung’s ongoing commitment to delivering comprehensive and proactive health management solutions through the advanced capabilities of Galaxy Watch.”</p>



<p>Samsung remains committed to researching how Galaxy Watch can support patients in managing their daily physical health. By fostering sustainable wellness habits, the company aims to help patients achieve better clinical outcomes and long-term vitality.</p>



<p>Samsung continues to expand its partnerships with leading medical institutions to advance wearable health monitoring capabilities and broaden the digital health ecosystem. Recently, Samsung demonstrated the potential for early vasovagal syncope (VVS) detection using Galaxy Watch in a <a href="https://bit.ly/4d7IfJJ" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">joint clinical study with Chung-Ang University Gwangmyeong Hospital in Korea</a> and also <a href="https://bit.ly/3YdvLJQ" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">collaborated with Stanford Medicine to further advance Galaxy Watch’s Sleep Apnea feature</a>.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/27151137/Samsung-Mobile-Massachusetts-General-Hospital-GLP-1-Treatment-Galaxy-Watch_Main1.jpg" alt="The logo of Samsung Health" class="wp-image-174433" /></figure>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="a6948455-d22d-439b-b090-6b340c841573">Glucagon-Like Peptide-1 (GLP-1) is a hormone secreted by the intestines after eating that regulates blood sugar levels and suppresses appetite. While GLP-1 weight-loss medications that mimic this hormone are gaining significant popularity globally, they can be accompanied by side effects such as gastrointestinal disorders, muscle mass loss and potential weight regain upon discontinuation. <a href="#a6948455-d22d-439b-b090-6b340c841573-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="a81a318c-73f3-4057-b456-f4bf42275456">The BioActive Sensor is a technology that integrates three sensors into a single chipset: an optical heart rate sensor (PPG), an electrical heart rate sensor (ECG) and a bioelectrical impedance analysis sensor (BIA). This sensor has been featured in Galaxy Watch devices since the release of Galaxy Watch4 in 2021, allowing users to measure and monitor various health indicators, such as body composition, heart rate, blood pressure and ECG tracking. <a href="#a81a318c-73f3-4057-b456-f4bf42275456-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 2"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="c186ca08-5a50-4a22-bca4-b759d1d3255e">DXA (Dual-Energy X-ray Absorptiometry) scan: A specialized medical imaging technology that uses low-dose X-rays to precisely measure body composition, including body fat, lean muscle mass and bone density. Universally recognized as the “gold standard” for body composition analysis, it is widely utilized in clinical research to accurately evaluate physiological changes. <a href="#c186ca08-5a50-4a22-bca4-b759d1d3255e-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 3"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li></ol>]]></content:encoded>

				<title><![CDATA[[Interview] The Future of Screen Experiences ①: Inside Samsung’s Micro RGB TV, Setting a New Standard for Next-Generation Displays]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/interview-the-future-of-screen-experiences-part-%e2%91%a0-inside-samsungs-micro-rgb-tv-setting-a-new-standard-for-next-generation-displays</link>
				<pubDate>Tue, 26 May 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/22173705/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Micro-RGB-TV-100-BT.2020-Micro-RGB-Color-Booster-Pro-AI-Soccer-Mode-Pro-Interview_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[TVs & Displays]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[AI Soccer Mode Pro]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Interview]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Micro RGB]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Micro RGB Color Booster Pro]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Supersize Picture Enhancer]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/3PhjPpp</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[From winning the CES 2026 Best of Innovation Award to being named one of TIME magazine’s “Best Inventions of the Year,” Samsung’s Micro RGB TV has earned global recognition. Building on its debut as the world’s first Micro RGB TV, Samsung Electronics is expanding the lineup this year with a 130-inch ultra-large model, setting a […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>From winning the CES 2026 Best of Innovation Award to being named one of TIME magazine’s “Best Inventions of the Year,” Samsung’s Micro RGB TV has earned global recognition. Building on its debut as the world’s first Micro RGB TV, Samsung Electronics is expanding the lineup this year with a 130-inch ultra-large model, setting a new benchmark for next-generation television technology.</p>



<p>From adopting micro-size RGB (red, green and blue) LEDs as a backlight unit to pursuing enhanced color expression and integrating AI technology for ultra-large displays, the development of the Micro RGB TV was a continuous series of firsts — with virtually no reference points to guide the process.</p>



<p>Samsung Newsroom spoke with Insang Hwang of the Visual Display (VD) Business Division’s Product Planning Group to learn more about how this new category of the Micro RGB TV was developed.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/22174736/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Micro-RGB-TV-100-BT.2020-Micro-RGB-Color-Booster-Pro-AI-Soccer-Mode-Pro-Interview_main1.jpg" alt="Micro RGB TV recognized for its technological excellence in the global market." class="wp-image-174385" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Micro RGB TV recognized for its technological excellence in the global market.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Creating a New Category With No Reference</strong></h2>



<p>The Micro RGB TV began as a project to create an entirely new category in the TV market. Hwang recalled, “Because the mission was to create a category that didn’t previously exist, every department — from development to sales and marketing — had to work together with a shared sense of urgency and responsibility.”</p>



<p>One of the biggest challenges was the absence of any reference point. The team had to develop new technologies and products from scratch while simultaneously defining the value they could deliver to consumers. “We went beyond simply applying RGB light sources,” he said. “We developed a proprietary concept called ‘Micro RGB,’ which miniaturized even the backlight unit itself to the micro level.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Pursuing 100% BT.2020 — The “Ultimate Color Gamut”</strong></h2>



<p>At the core of the Micro RGB TV is its color reproduction. By applying RGB LEDs as the backlight unit, the display achieves wide and highly accurate color reproduction.</p>



<p>“Although the Micro RGB TV started with the goal of delivering richer color reproduction, there was no clearly defined industry standard at the time,” Hwang said. “We felt a strong sense of responsibility, believing that the conditions we set could become the new standard for the market. That’s why we set the ambitious goal of achieving ‘100% BT.2020’ — the ultra-high-definition color standard defined by the International Telecommunication Union (ITU) and often referred to as the ‘ultimate color gamut.’”</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="656" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/22175113/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Micro-RGB-TV-100-BT.2020-Micro-RGB-Color-Booster-Pro-AI-Soccer-Mode-Pro-Interview_main2.jpg" alt="Micro RGB TV achieves 100% BT.2020 — the “ultimate color gamut” — setting a new standard in the TV market." class="wp-image-174387" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Micro RGB TV achieves 100% BT.2020 — the “ultimate color gamut” — setting a new standard in the TV market.</figcaption></figure>



<p>Achieving 100% BT.2020 means that a level of color reproduction once limited to professional monitors can now be experienced on TVs — one of the most widely used displays in everyday home environments. It also marks a significant advancement in the technical standards of the display industry.</p>



<p>The journey, however, was far from easy. “In the early stages of development, we struggled to reach the target values,” Hwang recalled. “However, through persistent efforts to achieve perfect color reproduction, the development team was ultimately able to meet its goal.” He added, “It wasn’t just about developing new technology. We also worked to establish measurable standards to validate its performance.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Bringing Cutting-Edge Technology Into Everyday Viewing</strong></h2>



<p>For product planners, the top priority is to convert advanced technology into an experience that users can easily perceive in everyday life. “We continuously thought about how to translate Micro RGB’s powerful hardware performance into a practical viewing experience,” Hwang said. “We focused on making its key strength — color — something users can feel naturally in everyday content while delivering an immersive viewing experience.”</p>



<p>“While Micro RGB achieves one of the highest color gamuts available in TVs today, only a limited amount of content fully utilizes it,” he noted. “So we enhanced software capabilities to ensure users can experience the difference across a wider range of content — from HDR content to everyday content such as OTT streaming and sports.”</p>



<p>One of the key features is <strong>Micro RGB Color Booster Pro</strong>. Hwang explained, “Leveraging a high-performance neural processing unit (NPU), AI analyzes content in real time to enhance color expression with precision. This allows users to enjoy Micro RGB’s vivid color performance not only in HDR content but also in everyday viewing.”</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="550" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/22175321/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Micro-RGB-TV-100-BT.2020-Micro-RGB-Color-Booster-Pro-AI-Soccer-Mode-Pro-Interview_main3.jpg" alt="Hwang explained that Micro RGB Color Booster Pro enhances color for a richer and more vivid viewing experience." class="wp-image-174388" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Hwang explained that Micro RGB Color Booster Pro enhances color for a richer and more vivid viewing experience.</figcaption></figure>



<p>He added, “For example, in soccer — one of the sports most frequently watched on TVs — the newly introduced <strong>AI Soccer Mode Pro</strong> automatically detects the content and enhances colors such as the grass and team uniforms. With the global football season kicking off in June, it’s a feature worth noting for those seeking a more immersive viewing experience.”</p>



<p>In addition, the TV incorporates a Glare Free feature designed for real-world viewing environments. “We applied glare-free technology so users can consistently enjoy Micro RGB’s exceptional color performance regardless of lighting conditions,” Hwang explained. “Whether in a dark room or a brightly lit space, viewers can stay fully immersed without reflections interfering with the screen.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Scaling Immersion With a 130-Inch Display</strong></h2>



<p>The newly introduced 130-inch ultra-large model delivers an overwhelming sense of immersion, as if the entire wall comes to life. As screen size increases, maintaining image detail becomes increasingly critical.</p>



<p>Hwang said, “We equipped the TV with <strong>Supersize Picture Enhancer</strong>, an AI-powered picture quality technology optimized for ultra-large displays. Thanks to this, viewers can enjoy Micro RGB’s rich colors and sharp image quality without distortion or pixelation.”</p>



<p>The sound experience and design were also significantly enhanced. “With a 160W 10.4.2-channel speaker system, the TV delivers immersive sound that fills the entire space without the need for external speakers,” he added.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="960" height="269" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/22175528/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Micro-RGB-TV-100-BT.2020-Micro-RGB-Color-Booster-Pro-AI-Soccer-Mode-Pro-Interview_main4.jpg" alt="Micro RGB TV features a wall-mount design that integrates seamlessly with the space, enhancing immersion." class="wp-image-174389" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Micro RGB TV features a wall-mount design that integrates seamlessly with the space, enhancing immersion.</figcaption></figure>



<p>The Micro RGB TV’s signature wall-mount design further reinforces immersion by blending the display seamlessly into its surroundings. “We developed a proprietary pocket structure and wall-mount bracket<sup data-fn="4b5cd42b-5cc0-4d39-8281-dd1b519cdae5" class="fn"><a href="#4b5cd42b-5cc0-4d39-8281-dd1b519cdae5" id="4b5cd42b-5cc0-4d39-8281-dd1b519cdae5-link">1</a></sup> so the TV can sit flush against the wall with virtually no gap,” Hwang explained. “We focused on delivering an optimized viewing experience for ultra-large screens across picture quality, sound and design.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Toward the Next-Generation Screen Experience</strong></h2>



<p>The Micro RGB TV goes beyond technological advancement — it expands the boundaries of how users experience screens in everyday life while setting new standards for the industry.</p>



<p>“Samsung TVs are evolving into screens that seamlessly integrate into users’ lifestyles and living spaces, understanding their preferences through data and enabling interactions,” Hwang said. “They will go beyond content consumption to become powerful platforms that connect limitless experiences and services.”</p>



<p>As the Micro RGB TV continues to push the boundaries of innovation, Samsung is paving the way for the next generation of screen experiences.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="4b5cd42b-5cc0-4d39-8281-dd1b519cdae5">Applicable to 85-, 75- and 65-inch models only <a href="#4b5cd42b-5cc0-4d39-8281-dd1b519cdae5-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li></ol>]]></content:encoded>

<p>Samsung Electronics is giving K-Pop fans a new way to experience the front-row energy of live SM Entertainment concerts from home — no ticket required. Building on the exclusive livestream of <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-tv-plus-to-exclusively-live-stream-smtown-live-2025-in-l-a-globally-on-new-smtown-channel" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">SMTOWN LIVE 2025 in L.A.</a>, <strong>Samsung TV Plus</strong> is expanding its collaboration with SM Entertainment to bring monthly concert broadcasts from popular SM artists to Samsung TVs and compatible Samsung devices through its subscription-free service.</p>



<p>The Monthly SM Concert series will be available exclusively on the <strong>SMTOWN channel</strong>, the Samsung TV Plus destination for SM Entertainment content. Available in Australia, New Zealand, Brazil, Mexico and Korea, the collaboration will bring premium K-Pop performances to growing fan communities in these markets.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>A Monthly K-Pop Stage, Built for Fans</strong></h2>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="321" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/21172502/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Samsung-TV-Plus-SMTOWN-Samsung-TVs-Monthly-SM-K-Pop-Concerts_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung TV Plus is expanding its collaboration with SM Entertainment." class="wp-image-174373" /></figure>



<p>To kick off the Monthly SM Concert series<strong>, NCT WISH’s </strong>first concert tour,<strong> “’INTO THE WISH: Our WISH’ ENCORE IN SEOUL,”</strong> will premiere live on <strong>Saturday, May 30 at 7 p.m. local time</strong>. Following the premiere, fans can tune in to the SMTOWN channel every Saturday at 7 p.m. for encore programming and future monthly concert streams, creating an easy weekend rhythm for watching SM performances from home.</p>



<p>With more SM artists and concert streams to be announced, the series will offer fresh performances and encore programming throughout the year, giving fans more ways to watch and revisit the artists they love on the biggest screen at home.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="837" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/21172521/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Samsung-TV-Plus-SMTOWN-Samsung-TVs-Monthly-SM-K-Pop-Concerts_main2.jpg" alt="Viewers can also use SmartThings on any smartphone or Samsung TVs to set reminders before each stream." class="wp-image-174374" /></figure>



<p>Viewers can also use SmartThings on any smartphone or Samsung TVs to set reminders before each stream, so they never miss a moment. For fans with compatible connected Samsung devices at home, SmartThings can help create a richer viewing environment by adjusting sound and lighting settings, bringing more of the concert atmosphere into the living room.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/21172538/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Samsung-TV-Plus-SMTOWN-Samsung-TVs-Monthly-SM-K-Pop-Concerts_main3.jpg" alt="NCT WISH’s first concert tour, “’INTO THE WISH: Our WISH’ ENCORE IN SEOUL,” will premiere live on Saturday, May 30." class="wp-image-174375" /></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>The Best Seat Is at Home</strong></h2>



<p>Samsung TV Plus continues to grow as a global destination for Korean entertainment, offering more than 4,000 hours of free-to-stream Korean content — from dramas, thrillers and romance to crime series, music programming and live event experiences.</p>



<p>The Monthly SM Concert series builds on this offering with monthly programming that lets fans follow every minute of their favorite SM performances from home, at no additional cost.</p>



<p>Made for everyone and every moment, Samsung TV Plus offers over 4,300 channels globally, subscription-free, and is available in 30 countries exclusively across Samsung TVs, Samsung Galaxy phones, XR headsets, Galaxy Tab, Smart Monitor and Family Hub lineups. This includes the new <a href="https://www.samsung.com/?r=true&referrer=usnewsroom" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">2026 TV series</a> announced earlier this year at CES, spanning Samsung Micro RGB TV, Neo QLED, OLED, The Frame, The Frame Pro and more.</p>



<p>More information on Samsung TV Plus is available at <a href="https://www.samsungtvplus.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">samsungtvplus.com</a>.</p>

<p>Technological advancements should benefit everyone equally. In line with this vision, Samsung Electronics is evolving beyond simply reducing the burden of household chores to become “a companion for everyone” that delivers greater convenience in everyday life. These efforts were recognized at the prestigious iF Design Awards 2026 and IDEA Awards 2025, where Samsung was honored for its accessibility-related features and inclusive design concepts.</p>



<p>Samsung continues to apply inclusive design across its home appliances by integrating a wide range of visual, auditory and sensory experiences. From older adults to users with disabilities, the company carefully considers even the smallest inconveniences users may encounter throughout every interaction with its products.</p>



<p>In particular, Samsung has extended Relumino outline — an accessibility feature designed to assist users with low vision — to screen-equipped appliances, helping them enjoy a consistent accessibility experience regardless of which Samsung device they use.</p>



<p>Additional features all contribute to a more inclusive appliance ecosystem. These include Auto Open Door, which opens doors with a simple voice command and Easy mode for more intuitive interaction with the Bespoke AI Laundry Combo’s 7-inch Smart Screen. Samsung also supports accessibility setting sync between screen-equipped appliances and smartphones, so users can enjoy a consistent experience across devices.</p>



<p>Check out the infographic below to explore the key accessibility features of Samsung AI appliances, which are designed to bring greater comfort and warmth to everyday life for everyone.</p>

<p>You’re finally on your long-awaited summer vacation in London, lining up the perfect shot of Tower Bridge with your Galaxy S26 Ultra. But just as you get the angle right, your phone slips and the screen touches on the pavement. </p>



<p>It’s every traveler’s worst nightmare and yet such accidents are more common than you think. According to <a href="https://www.samsung.com/sec/Samsung-Care-Plus/IM/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Samsung Care+</a><sup data-fn="4a0f7857-89ee-4b01-b40d-2f4dd0e3a898" class="fn"><a href="#4a0f7857-89ee-4b01-b40d-2f4dd0e3a898" id="4a0f7857-89ee-4b01-b40d-2f4dd0e3a898-link">1</a></sup> data, claims submitted in July and August were 30% higher than the annual average.<sup data-fn="1c1a95af-c396-4150-a3cd-c5b8614437ff" class="fn"><a href="#1c1a95af-c396-4150-a3cd-c5b8614437ff" id="1c1a95af-c396-4150-a3cd-c5b8614437ff-link">2</a></sup> With your phones holding everything from boarding passes and hotel reservations to maps, a damaged device could be a potential trip-ender.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/19102425/Samsung-Mobile-Samsung-Care-Galaxy-S26-Ultra-Summer-Vacation-London_main1.jpg" alt="Accidental damages during travel can cause a stressful situation." class="wp-image-174210" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Accidental damages during travel can cause a stressful situation.</figcaption></figure>

<p>First things first, there’s no need to panic or cancel travel plans. <ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>No Complex Paperwork: </strong>You can get support through a clear, easy-to-follow system without complicated paperwork.</li>



<li><strong>Priority</strong> <strong>Queue</strong><sup data-fn="c1e1a887-7bfb-4b5c-8a93-0821eed62106" class="fn"><a href="#c1e1a887-7bfb-4b5c-8a93-0821eed62106" id="c1e1a887-7bfb-4b5c-8a93-0821eed62106-link">4</a></sup><strong> Access: </strong>Once enrollment is verified, you’ll receive support with clear guidance.</li>

<p>Once the device is submitted for repair, Samsung-certified technicians take over. These professionals, who know Samsung Galaxy devices better than anyone, only use genuine parts<strong>. </strong>This ensures repairs go beyond fixing visible damage, returning devices to optimal condition so they maintain their performance and value.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/19102703/Samsung-Mobile-Samsung-Care-Galaxy-S26-Ultra-Summer-Vacation-London_main3.jpg" alt="All repairs are handled by certified experts using original parts." class="wp-image-174212" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ All repairs are handled by certified experts using original parts.</figcaption></figure>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung and Google Give First Look at New Intelligent Eyewear]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-and-google-give-first-look-at-new-intelligent-eyewear</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 20 May 2026 02:45:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/19171320/Samsung-Mobile-Intelligent-Eyewear-Google-Gentle-Monster-Warby-Parker-Gemini_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Mobile]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Release]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Gemini]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Gentle Monster]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Google]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Intelligent Eyewear]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Warby Parker]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4eRkIzj</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics and Google today unveiled new intelligent eyewear at Google I/O 2026 by giving a first look at two premium styles created with eyewear partners Gentle Monster and Warby Parker. Designed to work as a companion device to a mobile phone, the new eyewear enables users to access help through voice interaction and connect […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics and Google today unveiled new intelligent eyewear<sup data-fn="435e0485-0c10-44fe-80ec-ea51efa56796" class="fn"><a href="#435e0485-0c10-44fe-80ec-ea51efa56796" id="435e0485-0c10-44fe-80ec-ea51efa56796-link">1</a></sup> at Google I/O 2026 by giving a first look at two premium styles created with eyewear partners Gentle Monster and Warby Parker. Designed to work as a companion device to a mobile phone, the new eyewear enables users to access help through voice interaction and connect seamlessly to their phones, all through a familiar form factor.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/19165111/Samsung-Mobile-Intelligent-Eyewear-Google-Gentle-Monster-Warby-Parker-Gemini_main1.jpg" alt="Two premium intelligent eyewear designs from Gentle Monster and Warby Parker" class="wp-image-174246" /></figure>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/19165125/Samsung-Mobile-Intelligent-Eyewear-Google-Gentle-Monster-Warby-Parker-Gemini_main2.jpg" alt="Two premium intelligent eyewear designs from Gentle Monster and Warby Parker" class="wp-image-174247" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Two premium intelligent eyewear designs from Gentle Monster and Warby Parker</figcaption></figure>



<p>Co-created with the eyewear partners, the intelligent eyewear combines breakthrough AI capabilities with comfort and style, merging Samsung’s leadership in hardware engineering and Google’s AI technology with premium eyewear design. Each eyewear brand brings a distinct design approach to the device. Renowned for their legacies in fashion eyewear, Gentle Monster presents styles with disruptive yet refined aesthetics, while Warby Parker showcases refined and timeless designs.</p>



<p>Built to understand the world alongside users in real time, the new intelligent eyewear provides everyday support while keeping users hands-free and heads-up. Users can access navigation assistance by simply asking Gemini with their voices, receive personalized suggestions such as a nearby coffee shop on their walking route, or even place an order for pickup. Users can also receive summarized notifications for important texts and add events to their calendars. Additional features include real-time translations with audio that matches the speaker’s voice, as well as the ability to translate text on menus or signs in the user’s line of sight. Working seamlessly within the Galaxy ecosystem, the device helps users easily manage everyday tasks or effortlessly capture photos, all without taking their phone out.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="910" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/01102258/Samsung-Mobile-Intelligent-Eyewear-Google-Gentle-Monster-Warby-Parker-Gemini_main3F.jpg" alt="The design reflects Warby Parker's refined, timeless design." class="wp-image-174553" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ The design reflects Warby Parker’s refined, timeless design.</figcaption></figure>



<p>“This intelligent eyewear marks an important step in Samsung’s vision for AI,” said Jay Kim, Executive Vice President and Head of Customer Experience Office, Mobile eXperience (MX) Business at Samsung Electronics. “With this new AI form factor, we are further expanding the Galaxy device ecosystem, where each device is optimized to deliver unique AI experiences that best fit each form.”</p>



<p>“Intelligent eyewear represents a powerful step forward in our shared vision with Samsung to make AI more helpful and accessible in everyday life,” said Shahram Izadi, Vice President and GM of Android XR at Google. “Combining the best of Google’s AI and the Android ecosystem together with Samsung’s leadership in mobile hardware and Gentle Monster and Warby Parker’s premium design, we are helping users stay connected and fashionable in a more natural, hands-free way.”</p>



<p>“Intelligent eyewear should feel as emotionally expressive as it is technologically advanced,” said Hankook Kim, Founder and CEO of Gentle Monster. “Our vision was to merge fashion and technology in a way that feels bold, beautiful and human, bringing Gentle Monster’s disruptive design identity into a new era of intelligent eyewear with Samsung and Google.”</p>



<p>“Eyewear is deeply personal, which is why every detail matters when integrating advanced technology into frames people wear every day,” said Dave Gilboa, Co-Founder and Co-CEO of Warby Parker. “Our Intelligent Eyewear is designed to feel intuitive, combining Warby Parker’s signature design with precision optics and exceptional comfort to help people stay focused on the moments in front of them.”</p>



<p>The first collections of intelligent eyewear are scheduled to launch this fall in select markets, with additional details to be announced in the coming months.</p>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Launches Next-Gen Odyssey Gaming and ViewFinity Monitors, Including Industry’s First 6K Gaming Monitor]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-launches-next-gen-odyssey-gaming-and-viewfinity-monitors-including-industrys-first-6k-gaming-monitor</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 20 May 2026 00:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/18172728/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Next-Gen-Odyssey-Gaming-ViewFinity-Monitors-6K-Gaming-Monitor_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>

									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced the global availability of its latest Odyssey gaming monitors and ViewFinity S8 lineup, setting new benchmarks in resolution and performance across gaming and professional displays. Led by three Odyssey G8 models — including the industry’s first 6K gaming monitor — and complemented by the Odyssey G7 — which brings Samsung’s OLED […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics today announced the global availability of its latest Odyssey gaming monitors and ViewFinity S8 lineup, setting new benchmarks in resolution and performance across gaming and professional displays.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/18175130/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Next-Gen-Odyssey-Gaming-ViewFinity-Monitors-6K-Gaming-Monitor_Main1.jpg" alt="An Image of Odyssey G8 (G80HS model) " class="wp-image-174172" /></figure>



<p>Led by three Odyssey G8 models — including the industry’s first 6K gaming monitor — and complemented by the Odyssey G7 — which brings Samsung’s OLED technology to a broader range of users — the 2026 Odyssey lineup reinforces Samsung’s leadership in high-performance gaming displays while expanding access to advanced innovations.</p>



<p>This launch comes amid Samsung’s <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-retains-no-1-position-in-global-gaming-monitor-market-for-seventh-year" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">continued leadership</a> in the global gaming monitor market, where it holds an 18.9 percent revenue share. The company has also earned the No. 1 position in the OLED gaming monitor market for the third consecutive year with a 26 percent share, according to International Data Corporation (IDC).</p>



<p>“With the launch of the latest Odyssey and ViewFinity lineups, we continue to push the boundaries of performance and visual quality,” said Hun Lee, Executive Vice President of Visual Display (VD) Business at Samsung Electronics. “With our 2026 lineup, we are delivering our most advanced display technologies yet while expanding access, enabling more users to experience Samsung’s innovations across gaming and professional environments.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Odyssey G8: Setting a New Standard for High-Performance Gaming</strong></h2>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/18175218/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Next-Gen-Odyssey-Gaming-ViewFinity-Monitors-6K-Gaming-Monitor_Main2.jpg" alt="An Image of Odyssey G8 (G80HS model) " class="wp-image-174173" /></figure>



<p>The Odyssey G8 lineup introduces three state-of-the-art models designed to deliver high-performance experiences across a range of gaming scenarios.</p>



<p>The 32-inch Odyssey G8 (G80HS model) sets a new milestone as the industry’s first 6K gaming monitor, marking a significant leap beyond 4K gaming standards. 6K resolution presents exceptional visual clarity and detail, enhancing immersion while providing expanded screen space for both gaming and multitasking. It delivers ultra-high 6K resolution at 165Hz, while Dual Mode enables up to 330Hz at 3K resolution, allowing users to seamlessly balance immersive visual details with ultra-fast responsiveness.</p>



<p>Meanwhile, the 27-inch Odyssey G8 (G80HF model) offers flexible performance options, supporting 5K resolution at 180Hz or up to 360Hz in QHD through Dual Mode, making it suitable for both immersive and competitive gaming.</p>



<p>The Odyssey OLED G8 (G80SH model), available in 27-inch and 32-inch sizes, features an OLED panel with 4K resolution and a 240Hz refresh rate. Glare Free technology significantly reduces glare without compromising OLED picture quality. Connectivity options, including USB-C with up to 98W charging, support high-performance gaming setups. Moreover, the Odyssey OLED G8 adopts QD-OLED Penta Tandem technology, which significantly enhances efficiency, durability and brightness. The 32-inch Odyssey OLED G8 also received VESA DisplayHDR<img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/2122.png" alt="™" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" /> True Black 500 certification, delivering OLED’s deep blacks and vivid colors.</p>



<p>Across the lineup, DisplayPort 2.1<sup data-fn="e647303d-2410-48e8-8ff5-e624dfaa4d2c" class="fn"><a href="#e647303d-2410-48e8-8ff5-e624dfaa4d2c" id="e647303d-2410-48e8-8ff5-e624dfaa4d2c-link">1</a></sup> ensures high-bandwidth performance for next-generation visuals, while AMD FreeSync Premium and NVIDIA G-Sync Compatible technology deliver smooth, tear-free gameplay. Additionally, the Odyssey G8 lineup features HDR10+ GAMING,<sup data-fn="ea42f6a0-158c-4837-8502-5c1067bee121" class="fn"><a href="#ea42f6a0-158c-4837-8502-5c1067bee121" id="ea42f6a0-158c-4837-8502-5c1067bee121-link">2</a></sup> which dynamically optimizes brightness and contrast in real time.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Odyssey G7: Expanding Access to OLED Gaming</h2>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/18175308/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Next-Gen-Odyssey-Gaming-ViewFinity-Monitors-6K-Gaming-Monitor_Main3.jpg" alt="An Image of Odyssey  OLED G7 (G73SH model)" class="wp-image-174174" /></figure>



<p>The 32-inch Odyssey OLED G7 (G73SH model) expands Samsung’s OLED gaming lineup by bringing premium visual performance to a wider range of users.</p>



<p>It features 4K resolution and a 165Hz refresh rate, delivering detailed visuals and smooth gameplay. Dual Mode enables up to 330Hz in FHD, while a 0.03ms response time supports fast, responsive performance in competitive gaming environments.</p>



<p>With the addition of the G7, Samsung continues to extend its OLED gaming leadership while making advanced display technologies more widely accessible.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>ViewFinity S8: High-Resolution Displays for Professional Workflows</strong></h2>



<p>The ViewFinity S8 lineup is designed to meet the demands of modern professional environments, combining high-resolution clarity with advanced connectivity and ergonomic flexibility. Whether managing complex creative workflows or seamlessly multitasking across applications, these monitors are engineered to deliver a refined, high-performance experience that maximizes productivity.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/18175605/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Next-Gen-Odyssey-Gaming-ViewFinity-Monitors-6K-Gaming-Monitor_Main4.jpg" alt="An Image of the 40-inch ViewFinity S8 (S85TH model)" class="wp-image-174176" /></figure>



<p>The 40-inch ViewFinity S8 (S85TH model) features a curved WUHD display with a 144Hz refresh rate, enabling seamless multitasking and efficient handling of complex workflows. Thunderbolt 5 supports high-resolution video and data-intensive tasks with data transfer speeds of 80 Gbps and device charging up to 140W. In addition, Easy Connection provides streamlined connectivity across devices.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/18175642/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Next-Gen-Odyssey-Gaming-ViewFinity-Monitors-6K-Gaming-Monitor_Main5.jpg" alt="An Image of the 27-inch ViewFinity S8  (S80HF model)" class="wp-image-174177" /></figure>



<p>The 27-inch ViewFinity S8 (S80HF model) offers 5K resolution with USB-C connectivity for streamlined data transfer and device charging. Its ergonomic design supports comfortable long-term use and, since it is made to deliver 5K resolution in a more accessible package, it brings high-resolution performance to a broader range of professional users.</p>



<p>The new Odyssey G8 lineup, Odyssey G7 and ViewFinity S8 are available for order starting today. For more information, please visit <a href="http://www.samsung.com" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">www.samsung.com</a>.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="e647303d-2410-48e8-8ff5-e624dfaa4d2c">G80SH supports DisplayPort 2.1 UHBR20, delivering up to 80Gbps of bandwidth for smooth and uncompressed visuals. <a href="#e647303d-2410-48e8-8ff5-e624dfaa4d2c-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="ea42f6a0-158c-4837-8502-5c1067bee121">Compatible with HDMI 2.1 cables connected to the HDMI ports of NVIDIA and Intel GPUs. 									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced a new global collaboration between Samsung Art Store and Moomins, introducing an exclusive digital art collection featuring the iconic and beloved Moomin characters created by Finnish artist and writer Tove Jansson. Available on Samsung Art Store, the collection features a curated selection of 60 artworks designed to bring the wonderful world […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics today announced a new global collaboration between Samsung Art Store and Moomins, introducing an exclusive digital art collection featuring the iconic and beloved Moomin characters created by Finnish artist and writer Tove Jansson.</p>



<p>Available on Samsung Art Store, the collection features a curated selection of 60 artworks designed to bring the wonderful world of the Moomins and Moominvalley into millions of homes across the globe via Samsung Art TVs.</p>



<p>Known for their distinctive and enduring charm, the Moomins have remained a beloved global sensation for generations, with a legacy spanning publishing, animation and design. Through this partnership, Samsung Art Store continues to expand its offering of globally recognized content, giving users new ways to personalize their spaces through art and fan-favorite characters.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="491" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/15150013/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Art-Store-Moomins-Global-Collaboration_Main-1.jpg" alt="“Hattifatteners” (from “Finn Family Moomintroll” (1948)), by Tove Jansson on The Frame Pro" class="wp-image-174062" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ “Hattifatteners” (from “Finn Family Moomintroll” (1948)), by Tove Jansson on The Frame Pro</figcaption></figure>



<p>As more people look to make their homes feel more personal and expressive, Samsung Art Store is introducing collections that resonate — and the Moomins are a prime example. With this addition, users can now bring one of the world’s most loved fictional universes into their homes.</p>



<p>“The world of the Moomins has always reminded people of the importance of optimism, togetherness and finding beauty in everyday moments,” said Heeyeong Ahn, Vice President of the Visual Display Business at Samsung Electronics. “Through Samsung Art Store, we’re excited to bring that feeling into the home through a collection that is as immersive as it is inspiring.”</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="491" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/15150109/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Art-Store-Moomins-Global-Collaboration_Main-2.jpg" alt="“Garden Party” (from “The Dangerous Journey” (1977)) by Tove Jansson" class="wp-image-174063" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ “Garden Party” (from “The Dangerous Journey” (1977)) by Tove Jansson</figcaption></figure>



<p>The collection features a curated selection of original Moomin artwork spanning decades of storytelling and illustration. From Tove Jansson’s iconic black and white illustrations from the original novels in the 1940s to watercolor artwork from beloved picture books and cover illustrations, the collection celebrates the rich artistic legacy of the Moomins across generations. The collection also includes more recent interpretations of the Moomin world, serving to bring classic and contemporary works together in one experience.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="491" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/15150154/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-Art-Store-Moomins-Global-Collaboration_Main-3.jpg" alt="“The Floating Theatre” (from “Moominsummer Madness” (1982)) by Tove Jansson on The Fram" class="wp-image-174064" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ “The Floating Theatre” (from “Moominsummer Madness” (1954)) by Tove Jansson on The Frame</figcaption></figure>



<p>“At the heart of the Moomin stories is a sense of kindness, curiosity and emotional honesty that has resonated across generations around the world. In a fast-paced, hyper-optimised world, Moomin offers an alternative way of living for people hungry for meaning,” said James Zambra, Creative Director at Moomin Characters Oy Ltd. “Tove Jansson developed a fascinating visual language of considerable sophistication. We’re excited to partner with Samsung Art Store to introduce this enchanting world of the Moomins in a format that feels contemporary and naturally part of the home.”</p>



<p>Samsung Art TVs — including OLEDs<sup data-fn="cf40b687-5aea-45fc-ab5e-bc23749e6ebc" class="fn"><a href="#cf40b687-5aea-45fc-ab5e-bc23749e6ebc" id="cf40b687-5aea-45fc-ab5e-bc23749e6ebc-link">1</a></sup> now supported starting in 2026 — sit at the center of the experience, seamlessly displaying artwork in the modern home. Samsung Art Store’s growing collection spans genres and eras, redefining how art is discovered and experienced.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Availability</strong></h2>



<p>The Moomins collection will be available globally on Samsung Art Store from May 18.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h4 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>About Moomin</strong></h4>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">The Moomins first appeared in print in 1945 and went on to star in a series of books and comics, enthralling millions of readers all over the world. The stories about the adventurous and witty Moomins stem from the singular imagination of Tove Jansson (1914-2001), a Finnish-Swedish artist who created not only captivating tales but also a remarkable visual legacy. Her works span a vast spectrum of creativity, from intricate watercolour paintings to charming comic strips and illustrations. The Moomin stories, while accessible to all ages, delve into profound themes such as courage, our relationship with nature and the enduring power of friendship. The books have been translated into more than 60 languages. The Moomins have inspired stage adaptations, TV series, films, games, music, exhibitions and theme parks — and continue to take new forms.</h4>



<p></p>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading">Find out more about Tove Jansson and the Moomins here: </h4>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading"><a href="http://www.moomin.com" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">www.moomin.com</a></h4>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading"><a href="http://www.tovejansson.com" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">www.tovejansson.com</a></h4>

									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics is hosting its Australian Tech Summit 2026 in Sydney on May 14 and 15, offering media and industry professionals a deep dive into its latest AI-powered TV and an early look at its Odyssey gaming monitors ahead of their global rollout. The event features hands-on demonstrations highlighting how AI enhances picture quality, viewing […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics is hosting its Australian Tech Summit 2026 in Sydney on May 14 and 15, offering media and industry professionals a deep dive into its latest AI-powered TV and an early look at its Odyssey gaming monitors ahead of their global rollout.</p>



<p>The event features hands-on demonstrations highlighting how AI enhances picture quality, viewing experiences and display performance across Samsung’s Micro RGB, OLED and gaming displays.</p>



<p>The technologies showcased at the summit reflect Samsung’s long-standing leadership in the category, with the company ranking as the global TV market leader for 20 consecutive years.<sup data-fn="3e4d7422-9df9-4dce-9ef7-c722353dab4c" class="fn"><a href="#3e4d7422-9df9-4dce-9ef7-c722353dab4c" id="3e4d7422-9df9-4dce-9ef7-c722353dab4c-link">1</a></sup></p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="584" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14163614/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-AI-Powered-Screen-Innovations-Australia-Tech-Summit-2026_Main-1.jpg" alt="Media and industry professionals experience Samsung’s 2026 AI display innovations firsthand." class="wp-image-174006" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Media and industry professionals experience Samsung’s 2026 AI display innovations firsthand.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Micro RGB for Premium Home Viewing</strong></h2>



<p>A key focus of the event is Samsung’s new Micro RGB TV lineup, led by the flagship <strong>75-inch R95H and R85H</strong> models. Designed for premium home viewing, the lineup delivers precise color, deep contrast and an immersive picture quality.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14163733/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-AI-Powered-Screen-Innovations-Australia-Tech-Summit-2026_Main-2.jpg" alt="Samsung demonstrates the 75-inch Micro RGB TV (R95H) during a side-by-side picture quality comparison." class="wp-image-174007" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Samsung demonstrates the 75-inch Micro RGB TV (R95H) during a side-by-side picture quality comparison.</figcaption></figure>



<p>Samsung is also expanding Micro RGB technology with screen sizes ranging from 55 to 115 inches, bringing its core strengths — including rich color, sharp contrast and refined local dimming — to more home environments.</p>



<p>Powered by the Micro RGB AI Engine Pro, Samsung’s latest Micro RGB TVs optimize color and contrast in real time for lifelike detail. The lineup also achieves 100% of the BT.2020 color range and includes certified Glare Free technology to reduce reflections for a clearer viewing experience. Features such as Micro RGB Precision Color 100 and Vision AI Companion (VAC) further enhance picture quality and personalized viewing.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>OLED Innovation Powered by AI</strong></h2>



<p>Samsung’s 2026 OLED lineup combines cinematic picture quality, refined design and intelligent features to elevate the viewing experience. Leading the lineup is the <strong>77-inch S95H</strong>, which delivers brighter OLED performance, advanced HDR processing and a premium design that stands out even when the screen is off.</p>



<p>VAC brings AI to the center of the screen experience, offering a more natural way to interact with the TV and discover relevant content. Additional Samsung AI features further expand the OLED experience beyond picture quality.</p>



<p>AI Upscaling Pro improves low-resolution content by enhancing clarity, depth and contrast, while AI Soccer Mode Pro optimizes picture and sound for live sports and AI Sound Controller Pro gives viewers greater control over dialogue, background music, crowd noise and commentary.</p>



<p>HDR10+ Advanced technology delivers more precise brightness control, improved tone mapping and a more dynamic picture. Combined with certified Glare Free technology that minimizes reflections, the S95H maintains exceptional contrast and sharpness, even in bright spaces.</p>



<p>The S95H also features Samsung’s new FloatLayer Design for a lighter, gallery-inspired look. Art Mode and Samsung Art Store allow the TV to function as both a screen and a piece of home décor.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="641" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14163900/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-AI-Powered-Screen-Innovations-Australia-Tech-Summit-2026_Main-3.jpg" alt="Samsung presents its latest OLED innovations, including improvements in brightness, HDR performance and AI-based features." class="wp-image-174008" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Samsung presents its latest OLED innovations, including improvements in brightness, HDR performance and AI-based features.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Odyssey Gaming Monitors for Speed and Immersion</strong></h2>



<p>Samsung is expanding its Odyssey lineup with gaming monitors ranging from glasses-free 3D immersion to ultra-fast OLED performance and sharp 6K resolution.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="298" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14172029/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-AI-Powered-Screen-Innovations-Australia-Tech-Summit-2026_Main-4.jpg" alt="Samsung showcases its latest gaming monitor lineup — including OLED and 6K models." class="wp-image-174023" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Samsung showcases its latest gaming monitor lineup — including OLED and 6K models.</figcaption></figure>



<p>Leading the lineup is the <strong>27-inch Odyssey 3D (G90XF model)</strong>, featuring Eye Tracking and View Mapping technology for natural, glasses-free 3D immersion. With a 165Hz refresh rate and 1ms GtG<sup data-fn="ed4f0d75-fe8f-4005-b58b-3c014176e44e" class="fn"><a href="#ed4f0d75-fe8f-4005-b58b-3c014176e44e" id="ed4f0d75-fe8f-4005-b58b-3c014176e44e-link">2</a></sup> response time, it delivers smooth, responsive gameplay.</p>



<p>Also on display is the <strong>32-inch Odyssey G8 (G80HS model)</strong>, the industry’s first 6K gaming monitor offering a native 165Hz refresh rate, Dual Mode support up to 330Hz in 3K and VESA-certified DisplayPort 2.1 connectivity.</p>



<p>Samsung’s OLED gaming monitor lineup further expands performance with the <strong>32-inch Odyssey OLED G8 (G80SH model)</strong>, delivering 4K QD-OLED visuals at 240Hz. Samsung OLED Safeguard+ technology also helps maintain long-lasting picture quality.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14172627/Samsung-TVs-and-Display-AI-Powered-Screen-Innovations-Australia-Tech-Summit-2026_Main-5.jpg" alt="" class="wp-image-174025" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Andrew Sohn, Senior Engineer, Samsung Electronics, presents the Odyssey OLED G8 monitor, giving attendees the opportunity to experience its advanced display performance.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Shaping the Next Era of Screens</strong></h2>



<p>“Samsung’s 2026 display lineup combines the features consumers value most in TVs and monitors, including stunning picture quality, thoughtful design and AI features that make screens more personal and intuitive,” said Hun Lee, Executive Vice President of Visual Display (VD) Business at Samsung Electronics. “Across the lineup, Samsung is delivering a more complete screen experience for how people watch, play and work every day.”</p>



<p>With its 2026 portfolio, Samsung is expanding advanced screen technologies and AI features across a broader range of products and price points. From home entertainment and gaming to everyday productivity, the lineup reflects a future in which screens are smarter, sharper and more personalized than ever.</p>

																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics is hosting Samsung AI Week 2026 from May 11 to June 7 in 58 countries.<sup data-fn="0130b55f-a8d5-4a9e-a4c1-83c64ec85cc5" class="fn"><a href="#0130b55f-a8d5-4a9e-a4c1-83c64ec85cc5" id="0130b55f-a8d5-4a9e-a4c1-83c64ec85cc5-link">1</a></sup></p>



<p>Now in its seventh year, Samsung Week has become the company’s largest annual global promotion, celebrating its founding anniversary and thanking customers for their continued support with exclusive deals on a wide range of products. Beginning this year, the promotion is being held twice annually under the new name “Samsung AI Week.”</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="444" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14094948/Samsung-Corporate-Samsung-AI-Week-2026-Your-Companion-to-AI-Living.-The-everyday-effortless_main1F.jpg" alt="Samsung Electronics is hosting Samsung AI Week 2026 from May 11 to June 7 in 58 countries" class="wp-image-173972" /></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>AI-Powered Experiences for Everyday Living</strong></h2>



<p>The theme for Samsung AI Week 2026 is ‘Your Companion to AI Living. The everyday, effortless.’ Reflecting Samsung’s vision for its AI lineup — including Galaxy AI for mobile, Samsung Vision AI for TVs and Bespoke AI for home appliances — the campaign underscores how Samsung’s AI experiences help make everyday life easier, more intuitive and more connected.</p>



<p>The promotion features a broad range of Samsung products, including the latest releases such as the Galaxy S26 series, Galaxy Buds4 Pro, Mini LED TV, Q-Series Soundbar and Bespoke AI Laundry Combo.<sup data-fn="b2d843e3-c064-4482-b96a-4c1bf6d65b94" class="fn"><a href="#b2d843e3-c064-4482-b96a-4c1bf6d65b94" id="b2d843e3-c064-4482-b96a-4c1bf6d65b94-link">2</a></sup></p>



<p>To help users discover a more seamless AI-powered lifestyle, Samsung is also highlighting platforms that complement its devices, including Samsung Health, Samsung TV Plus and SmartThings. Through dedicated pages on <a href="https://www.samsung.com/sec/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Samsung.com</a>, visitors can explore additional ways to enhance their Samsung AI experience.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Personalized Recommendations for Everyday Living</strong></h2>



<p>For customers who opt in to marketing, the “Recommended Picks Tailored for You” section provides product suggestions based on owned devices and user activity, helping them discover options best suited to their needs and interests.<sup data-fn="9fd3f523-42dc-4e37-9a5d-3ec783b8ad87" class="fn"><a href="#9fd3f523-42dc-4e37-9a5d-3ec783b8ad87" id="9fd3f523-42dc-4e37-9a5d-3ec783b8ad87-link">3</a></sup></p>



<p>Samsung.com will also spotlight curated product selections built around three key lifestyle categories — Care Companion, Entertainment Companion and Home Companion. Designed around everyday scenarios, the featured products support experiences such as building personalized workout routines, enabling more immersive sports viewing and helping users create a smarter home for major life moments like moving or marriage.<sup data-fn="132cef7d-39bd-4bfb-8155-68d8d93c657e" class="fn"><a href="#132cef7d-39bd-4bfb-8155-68d8d93c657e" id="132cef7d-39bd-4bfb-8155-68d8d93c657e-link">4</a></sup></p>



<p>In addition, the “Complete Your AI Setup” section introduces recommended cross-category product combinations, allowing customers already using Samsung products to experience a more connected ecosystem. Organized by product type — such as Galaxy mobile devices, TVs and home appliances — the section highlights products commonly used together.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Enhanced Rewards Throughout Samsung AI Week</strong></h2>



<p>During the promotional period, customers who purchase products on Samsung.com can earn extra<sup data-fn="0ee32857-c52a-458f-89ba-75e2169e82fe" class="fn"><a href="#0ee32857-c52a-458f-89ba-75e2169e82fe" id="0ee32857-c52a-458f-89ba-75e2169e82fe-link">5</a></sup> Samsung Rewards points redeemable across a range of platforms, including Samsung.com, Galaxy Store and Samsung Art Store.<sup data-fn="e2d3609d-bbed-46c8-922f-1490d3ba4c3b" class="fn"><a href="#e2d3609d-bbed-46c8-922f-1490d3ba4c3b" id="e2d3609d-bbed-46c8-922f-1490d3ba4c3b-link">6</a></sup> Customers can also check their remaining points on the Samsung AI Week 2026 page throughout the event.<sup data-fn="344bb2a0-1319-4f93-8087-9a804877b197" class="fn"><a href="#344bb2a0-1319-4f93-8087-9a804877b197" id="344bb2a0-1319-4f93-8087-9a804877b197-link">7</a></sup></p>



<p>More information about Samsung AI Week 2026 is available on Samsung.com in each region. The campaign is appearing on digital billboards at major global landmarks, including Times Square in New York and Piccadilly Circus in London, from May 11 to June 7.<sup data-fn="01179c7e-49cd-4065-8484-fbc342c9f61f" class="fn"><a href="#01179c7e-49cd-4065-8484-fbc342c9f61f" id="01179c7e-49cd-4065-8484-fbc342c9f61f-link">8</a></sup></p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="980" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/14095046/Samsung-Corporate-Samsung-AI-Week-2026-Your-Companion-to-AI-Living.-The-everyday-effortless_main2F.jpg" alt="Samsung AI Week 2026 campaign in New York City" class="wp-image-173973" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Samsung AI Week 2026 campaign in New York City</figcaption></figure>
