				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Adopts New EU Code of Conduct for Energy Smart Appliances]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-adopts-new-eu-code-of-conduct-for-energy-smart-appliances</link>
				<pubDate>Thu, 14 May 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/13151309/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-EU-Code-Energy-Smart-Appliances_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Home Appliances]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Release]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[European Union]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Home Appliance]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Smart Appliances]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4uj5Tdq</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced that it has signed the European Union’s (EU) Code of Conduct (CoC) for interoperability and Energy Smart Appliances (ESAs). The CoC aims to accelerate the rollout of connected appliances that can work seamlessly with energy systems and help households use electricity more efficiently. “Samsung believes connected appliances can play a meaningful […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="491" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/13151325/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-EU-Code-Energy-Smart-Appliances_Main1.jpg" alt="An image of Bespoke AI Laundry Combo" class="wp-image-173946" /></figure>



<p>Samsung Electronics today announced that it has signed the European Union’s (EU) Code of Conduct (CoC) for interoperability and Energy Smart Appliances (ESAs). The CoC aims to accelerate the rollout of connected appliances that can work seamlessly with energy systems and help households use electricity more efficiently.</p>



<p>“Samsung believes connected appliances can play a meaningful role in the energy transition by helping households use energy more intelligently, without adding complexity to everyday life,” said Hyesoon Yang, Executive Vice President for the Digital Appliances (DA) New Biz Team at Samsung Electronics. “By joining this EU initiative, we aim to help make energy-smart functionality more accessible to consumers.”</p>



<p>Developed with manufacturers by the European Commission’s <a href="https://commission.europa.eu/about/departments-and-executive-agencies/joint-research-centre_en" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Joint Research Centre (JRC)</a> and <a href="https://commission.europa.eu/about/departments-and-executive-agencies/energy_en" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Directorate-General (DG) for Energy</a>, the CoC promotes cross-brand interoperability by defining common energy-related services and the information needed to enable them, even when different communication protocols are used. It covers a variety of energy-labeled appliances, such as major white goods and HVAC categories.</p>



<p>In line with the initiative’s timelines, Samsung combo, washer and dishwasher models that meet the CoC requirements have been registered in the European Product Registry for Energy Labelling (EPREL) as ESAs. These models support the Optimal Scheduling<sup data-fn="4c978083-3edf-4233-8ef7-79e95d84df24" class="fn"><a href="#4c978083-3edf-4233-8ef7-79e95d84df24" id="4c978083-3edf-4233-8ef7-79e95d84df24-link">1</a></sup> feature within SmartThings Energy,<sup data-fn="956ad576-11f6-4239-a058-5acdddc5270b" class="fn"><a href="#956ad576-11f6-4239-a058-5acdddc5270b" id="956ad576-11f6-4239-a058-5acdddc5270b-link">2</a></sup> enabling appliances to operate during off-peak hours. Additionally, SmartThings Energy allows users to monitor and manage energy consumption through the SmartThings app.</p>



<p>Looking forward, Samsung plans to gradually expand its lineup of products that comply with CoC requirements and continue contributing to efficient energy use.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="491" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/13151343/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-EU-Code-Energy-Smart-Appliances_Main2.jpg" alt="An image of Bespoke AI Dishwasher " class="wp-image-173947" /></figure>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="4c978083-3edf-4233-8ef7-79e95d84df24">Available in countries such as those in Europe where peak-time pricing is applied. Availability and benefits may vary by electricity provider and tariff conditions. Optimal Scheduling is set by the user in SmartThings Energy during peak-time settings. The device notifies the user of peak times and allows them to choose when to start. For home appliances without screens, users can check Optimal Scheduling status through an LED indicator. <a href="#4c978083-3edf-4233-8ef7-79e95d84df24-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="956ad576-11f6-4239-a058-5acdddc5270b">Available on Android and iOS devices. A Wi-Fi connection and a Samsung account are required. <a href="#956ad576-11f6-4239-a058-5acdddc5270b-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 2"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li></ol>]]></content:encoded>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung To Launch 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo, Advancing All-in-One Comfort Lifestyle]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-to-launch-2026-bespoke-ai-laundry-combo-advancing-all-in-one-comfort-lifestyle</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 13 May 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/13154836/Samsung-Home-Appliances-2026-Bespoke-AI-Laundry-Combo-All-In-One_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Home Appliances]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Release]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Bespoke AI]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Bespoke AI Laundry Combo]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Bixby]]></category>

									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced the upcoming launch of the 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo, an upgrade to its all-in-one laundry solution that has helped create a more comfortable lifestyle at home by eliminating the need to transfer laundry between separate machines. Following the product’s unveiling at CES in January, Samsung is now sharing full launch […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/13154835/Samsung-Home-Appliances-2026-Bespoke-AI-Laundry-Combo-All-In-One_Main1.jpg" alt="An image of Bespoke AI Laundry " class="wp-image-173958" /></figure>



<p>Samsung Electronics today announced the upcoming launch of the 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo,<sup data-fn="12cb6bc7-5d8d-4fca-82ca-bbf551b67b0f" class="fn"><a href="#12cb6bc7-5d8d-4fca-82ca-bbf551b67b0f" id="12cb6bc7-5d8d-4fca-82ca-bbf551b67b0f-link">1</a></sup> an upgrade to its all-in-one laundry solution that has helped create a more comfortable lifestyle at home by eliminating the need to transfer laundry between separate machines.</p>



<p>Following the product’s <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-to-unveil-new-ai-connected-living-lineup-at-ces-2026" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">unveiling</a> at CES in <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/ces-2026-a-home-companion-making-daily-life-more-effortless" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">January</a>, Samsung is now sharing full launch details — including faster wash-to-dry performance, an upgraded AI cycle and a more advanced voice experience — to highlight the improvements of the 2026 model.</p>



<p>“Since its debut, the Bespoke AI Laundry Combo has helped simplify one of the most repetitive household routines through true all-in-one convenience,” said Hyoung Min Park, VP and Head of the Customer Experience Team for the Digital Appliances (DA) Business at Samsung Electronics. “With the 2026 model, we’re building on that comfort lifestyle with upgrades that make laundry faster, smarter and easier to manage — while expanding options to meet a wider range of customer needs.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Faster Full Cycles, Enhanced Drying and Smarter Care</strong></h2>



<p>Following its 2024 debut, the 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo is launching with upgrades that shorten wash-to-dry cycles and enhance drying performance. Under specific conditions, the Super Speed cycle can complete a full wash-to-dry cycle in less time than the previous ventless combos,<sup data-fn="19a1e779-8090-4850-b6b6-60a15034c97b" class="fn"><a href="#19a1e779-8090-4850-b6b6-60a15034c97b" id="19a1e779-8090-4850-b6b6-60a15034c97b-link">2</a></sup> helping users reduce total laundry time without compromising performance.<sup data-fn="43f3813d-948c-4f61-8f43-7a45320f9fa8" class="fn"><a href="#43f3813d-948c-4f61-8f43-7a45320f9fa8" id="43f3813d-948c-4f61-8f43-7a45320f9fa8-link">3</a></sup></p>



<p>Super Speed leverages a high-pressure Speed Spray that improves detergent penetration and rinsing to enable fast and efficient washing, while the newly incorporated booster heat exchanger delivers improved drying performance. The upgraded combo also features Auto Open Door+,<sup data-fn="76309cc2-8f81-4564-8fb1-7cc3aa0e3bbd" class="fn"><a href="#76309cc2-8f81-4564-8fb1-7cc3aa0e3bbd" id="76309cc2-8f81-4564-8fb1-7cc3aa0e3bbd-link">4</a></sup> which not only automatically opens the door, but also activates internal air circulation<sup data-fn="c4c87c74-1c4e-4d62-a3b1-555b71601df5" class="fn"><a href="#c4c87c74-1c4e-4d62-a3b1-555b71601df5" id="c4c87c74-1c4e-4d62-a3b1-555b71601df5-link">5</a></sup> after wash-only cycles to help prevent laundry left in the drum from developing a musty odor.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Upgraded AI Wash & Dry + Enables More Precise, Automatic Optimization</strong></h2>



<p>At the core of the all-in-one experience, the 2026 model integrates AI Wash & Dry +,<sup data-fn="eb551123-3147-42aa-b04d-82639eab0ec8" class="fn"><a href="#eb551123-3147-42aa-b04d-82639eab0ec8" id="eb551123-3147-42aa-b04d-82639eab0ec8-link">6</a></sup> upgrading the intelligence that supports smart optimization of washing & drying. Using enhanced sensing and AI-based analysis, AI Wash & Dry + uses multiple sensors to optimize performance for each load. It detects the weight to determine the right amount of water and detergent, identifies five fabric types for smaller laundry loads<sup data-fn="dc855d3b-5c66-4709-9ae8-bed5682a1e3c" class="fn"><a href="#dc855d3b-5c66-4709-9ae8-bed5682a1e3c" id="dc855d3b-5c66-4709-9ae8-bed5682a1e3c-link">7</a></sup> — including Outdoor and Denim — and monitors soil levels in real time to adjust the cycle for better results with less manual input.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>A More Advanced Bixby Brings Natural, Conversational Control to the Home</strong></h2>



<p>Samsung is also bringing a more advanced Bixby<sup data-fn="7ca85f35-4171-468e-9e1a-cb33cf10def9" class="fn"><a href="#7ca85f35-4171-468e-9e1a-cb33cf10def9" id="7ca85f35-4171-468e-9e1a-cb33cf10def9-link">8</a></sup> experience to the 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo. Bixby has enabled users to monitor and control connected Samsung devices directly from a single appliance,<sup data-fn="075c900b-4602-4f25-b512-75a987b5cc1c" class="fn"><a href="#075c900b-4602-4f25-b512-75a987b5cc1c" id="075c900b-4602-4f25-b512-75a987b5cc1c-link">9</a></sup> making it easier to handle everyday routines across the home. While loading laundry, a user could say, “Start the robot vacuum in the living room” or “Turn on the air purifier,” without needing to unlock their phone or leave the laundry area.</p>



<p>Now, with improved understanding capabilities, Bixby goes beyond fixed commands to understand natural, conversational requests. For example, users can simply say, “Can you wash this before 11 p.m.?” or “Start a normal wash, but add an extra rinse,” and Bixby will understand and carry out the request.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Availability</strong></h2>



<p>To meet different regional needs and broaden consumer choice, Samsung will roll out the 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo with lineup options that vary by market. In select regions, Samsung will also introduce more affordable model options,<sup data-fn="37ca3bd4-9911-44c1-91f7-151a0272b273" class="fn"><a href="#37ca3bd4-9911-44c1-91f7-151a0272b273" id="37ca3bd4-9911-44c1-91f7-151a0272b273-link">10</a></sup> expanding availability across price segments while maintaining the core all-in-one convenience. As such, the 2026 Bespoke AI Laundry Combo will roll out in select markets throughout 2026.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />

																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics today announced the One UI 9 beta program, launching this week beginning with the Galaxy S26 series. Built on the new Android 17, One UI 9 beta delivers expanded creative tools, customization options, a more accessible mobile experience and stronger protection against potential security threats.</p>



<p>The full experience of One UI 9 will be introduced with upcoming Galaxy flagship devices later this year, which will include advanced AI features that will make mobile interaction easy and effortless.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>What’s New in One UI 9 Beta</strong></h2>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="560" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/12152351/Samsung-Mobile-One-UI-9-Beta-Galaxy-S26-series_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung Electronics today announced the One UI 9 beta program, launching this week beginning with the Galaxy S26 series." class="wp-image-173900" /></figure>



<p>One UI 9 beta introduces several updates across key areas of the mobile experience.</p>



<p><strong>Samsung Notes</strong><sup data-fn="1f8ce992-b43b-45b5-be46-45ac79693420" class="fn"><a href="#1f8ce992-b43b-45b5-be46-45ac79693420" id="1f8ce992-b43b-45b5-be46-45ac79693420-link">1</a></sup> gains creative new tools, including decorative tapes and a wider variety of pen line styles. Meanwhile, the <strong>Contacts</strong> app now offers direct access to Creative Studio<sup data-fn="2088bdc9-4322-4172-b2c6-b03807b44a7f" class="fn"><a href="#2088bdc9-4322-4172-b2c6-b03807b44a7f" id="2088bdc9-4322-4172-b2c6-b03807b44a7f-link">2</a></sup> for creating personalized profile cards without the need to switch between apps.</p>



<p>The updated <strong>Quick Panel</strong><sup data-fn="bf87713d-60bb-47dc-b0f2-a2a70ef33db1" class="fn"><a href="#bf87713d-60bb-47dc-b0f2-a2a70ef33db1" id="bf87713d-60bb-47dc-b0f2-a2a70ef33db1-link">3</a></sup> gives users greater control over its layout. Brightness, sound and media player are each independently adjustable, with more size options to suit individual preferences.</p>



<p>Accessibility is significantly improved by an adjustable <strong>Mouse Key</strong> speed that enables smoother cursor control and a combined <strong>TalkBack</strong> package that brings together features previously offered separately by Google and Samsung. The new <strong>Text Spotlight</strong> feature — which displays selected text larger or more clearly in a floating window — has also been added to make reading easier.</p>



<p>One UI 9 also introduces enhanced protection against suspicious apps and potential threats: when new high-risk apps are detected, it now warns users, blocks execution and installation, and recommends deletion through security policy updates.<sup data-fn="8773ee5d-30ab-4f2c-b86a-18e4f2323ed7" class="fn"><a href="#8773ee5d-30ab-4f2c-b86a-18e4f2323ed7" id="8773ee5d-30ab-4f2c-b86a-18e4f2323ed7-link">4</a></sup></p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Availability</strong></h2>



<p>The One UI 9 beta program will be available to Galaxy S26 series users in select markets, including Germany, India, Korea, Poland, the U.K. and the U.S starting this week. Galaxy S26 series users can apply to join the beta program via the Samsung Members app.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="1f8ce992-b43b-45b5-be46-45ac79693420">Service availability may vary by region/country, OS/One UI version, device model and phone carrier. <a href="#1f8ce992-b43b-45b5-be46-45ac79693420-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="2088bdc9-4322-4172-b2c6-b03807b44a7f">Requires Creative Studio app installation. Creative Studio feature requires a network connection and Samsung Account login. Service availability may vary by country, language or device model. The accuracy and reliability of the generated output is not guaranteed. Sticker can only be shared with other Galaxy devices. <a href="#2088bdc9-4322-4172-b2c6-b03807b44a7f-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 2"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="bf87713d-60bb-47dc-b0f2-a2a70ef33db1">Certain settings might be grayed out or will not appear if the feature is turned off. <a href="#bf87713d-60bb-47dc-b0f2-a2a70ef33db1-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 3"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li><li id="8773ee5d-30ab-4f2c-b86a-18e4f2323ed7">Samsung’s security policy updates are designed to improve device security through service operation policy changes and may include updates to list of potential high-risk apps according to Samsung’s internal assessment.  <a href="#8773ee5d-30ab-4f2c-b86a-18e4f2323ed7-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 4"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li></ol>]]></content:encoded>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Solve for Tomorrow Wins Merit Award at 2026 Global Views ESG Corporate Sustainability Awards]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-solve-for-tomorrow-wins-merit-award-at-2026-global-views-esg-corporate-sustainability-awards</link>
				<pubDate>Tue, 12 May 2026 00:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/themes/newsroom/images/default_image.png" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Worldwide]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4nxLtev</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Solve for Tomorrow was recently honored with the Merit Award in the Education Promotion category at the 2026 Global Views ESG Corporate Sustainability Awards. This recognition comes after the program has earned widespread acclaim from educators and students alike for its robust training framework since its 2020 debut in Taiwan. Organized by Global Views […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/15134102/Samsung-CSR-Samsung-Solve-for-Tomorrow-Merit-Award-2026-ESG_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung Solve for Tomorrow was recently honored with the Merit Award." class="wp-image-174038" /></figure>



<p>Samsung Solve for Tomorrow was recently honored with the Merit Award in the Education Promotion category at the 2026 Global Views ESG Corporate Sustainability Awards. This recognition comes after the program has earned widespread acclaim from educators and students alike for its robust training framework since its 2020 debut in Taiwan.</p>



<p>Organized by Global Views Monthly, the award evaluates corporate performance across environmental, social and governance (ESG) dimensions, honoring organizations that demonstrate a profound, long-term commitment to sustainable development. The award highlights Samsung’s efforts to advance sustainability education through a scalable model that bridges classroom learning with real-world impact.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/15134124/Samsung-CSR-Samsung-Solve-for-Tomorrow-Merit-Award-2026-ESG_main2.jpg" alt="By leveraging a structured Design Thinking framework, participants apply academic learning to real-world challenges." class="wp-image-174039" /></figure>



<p>Solve for Tomorrow equips students with the tools and mindset to address real-world challenges. The program specifically engages students aged 15 to 18, recognizing that this is a pivotal stage where strong technical aptitude meets the formation of personal values and social perspectives. By leveraging a structured Design Thinking framework, participants apply academic learning to real-world challenges and develop solutions that yield tangible social impact.</p>



<p>The program continues to expand through initiatives such as Corporate Sustainability Tours and Environmental Education, alongside Coaching Workshops aimed at elevating educator capabilities. In 2026, the curriculum was bolstered by hands-on AI training and the Alumni Engagement Program to accelerate idea development and facilitate ongoing peer exchange.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="321" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/15134132/Samsung-CSR-Samsung-Solve-for-Tomorrow-Merit-Award-2026-ESG_main3.jpg" alt="The program continues to expand through initiatives such as Corporate Sustainability Tours, Environmental Education and Coaching Workshops." class="wp-image-174040" /></figure>



<p>Solve for Tomorrow participants have demonstrated measurable growth across essential 21st-century competencies, including critical thinking, collaborative problem-solving and creative innovation. Educators who mentor these teams also report meaningful changes, noting that students demonstrate stronger self-directed learning and communication skills after completing the program.</p>



<p><a href="https://news.samsung.com/tw/%E5%8F%B0%E7%81%A3%E4%B8%89%E6%98%9F%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90-solve-for-tomorrow-%E6%A6%AE%E7%8D%B22026%E5%B9%B4%E9%81%A0%E8%A6%8Besg%E4%BC%81%E6%A5%AD%E6%B0%B8%E7%BA%8C%E7%8D%8E" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Learn more at Samsung Taiwan Newsroom</a></p>
